You should have bought an X-Box One</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">\n<span class="a-size-normal">\n<span class="a-color-secondary">\n      By\n    </span>\n<a class="noTextDecoration" href="/gp/pdp/profile/ARPJAQZHMOV4C">Erik Setzer</a>\n</span>\n<span class="a-color-secondary"> on August 28, 2015</span></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small" id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R3HB7RD8Z62G4"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Platform for Display: Xbox 360</span>\n<div class="a-section">\n  Were you excited by all the new features and changes mentioned all over the Internet, in previews and reviews, in videos everywhere?<br><br>Too bad.  You should have bought an X-Box One.<br><br>There is no new scouting system in Madden 16 on the X-Box 360.  Instead, you get the new points (fewer points, losing points if you sim ahead without scouting every week), but you get the old system with a bonus (I mean, other than the lack of points making it hard to skim the surface of a tiny number of players): It\'s bugged.  Every player shows Strength as "fully scouted" with a 0.  Which is just the kind of thing that really helps you figure out which offensive or defensive lineman you want to select!<br><br>The new passing style might be there, but it\'s hard to tell at times, when passes seem to go anywhere but where you wanted them to.  There is a tutorial on it, though.<br><br>Draft Champions is there, and that at least seems like an interesting way to play the game.  Is it worth $60 (or $70 for Deluxe Edition)?  Not at all.<br><br>It\'s one thing to see minor changes from edition to edition with Madden.  We get that.  They remove features because it\'s easier to do that than develop them, or they can add them back later and pretend they\'re new (like owner mode).  But having an edition of the game where they manage to break more than they add while simultaneously having the "same" edition on another system with a lot more features?  We\'re getting into new territory here.<br><br>If you have a 360, you\'ve just been told you\'re an afterthought by EA.  Make them an afterthought in your own mind.  Don\'t buy this game on X-Box 360.\n</br></br></br></br></br></br></br></br></br></br></br></br></div>\n</div>\n<a class="a-link-normal comment-link commentStripe" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R3HB7RD8Z62G4" title="1">1 Comment</a>\n<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator commentStripe"></i>\n<a id="R3HB7RD8Z62G4.2115.Helpful.Reviews"></a>\n<span class="votingStripe" id="cr-vote-R3HB7RD8Z62G4">\n<span class="a-size-base a-color-secondary cr-vote-buttons">\n    6 of 8 people found this helpful.
